```

Pose
Kneeling upright on bed, knees together. Torso facing mirror. Head slightly tilted down toward phone. Right hand holding phone, left hand resting behind on mattress.

Cozy, dreamy mood. Palette: white, slate grey, soft pink, cool daylight blue.

Lighting

Environment

**Author**: [Kashberg](https://x.com/Kashberg_0)  **Date**: 2026-03-06  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，指示模型将半身像渲染成彩绘木雕或树脂雕塑。它指定了工具痕迹、凿刻平面、僵硬的雕塑头发（非写实）以及硬化彩绘的织物，并在柔和的博物馆灯光下拍摄。

![彩绘木雕肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772864613645_w86kld_HCsGPXzakAAejuQ.jpg)
![彩绘木雕肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772864613619_z0p4fc_HCsGPXxaUAEy9c-.jpg)
![彩绘木雕肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772864613667_ti4kj1_HCsGPXtawAA_m85.jpg)
![彩绘木雕肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772864614389_j0ez1l_HCsGPXyasAA8i3-.jpg)

```
SCULPTURE MATERIAL
The subject is carved from painted wood or resin (polychrome sculpture style).

Skin is no longer skin:
It becomes a matte carved surface with visible tool marks, tiny cracks, subtle paint wear, and hardened edges.

Add:
• chisel planes on cheeks and forehead
• carved eyelids and nostrils
• slightly flattened planes instead of soft flesh
• painted but slightly aged coloration

HAIR (CRITICAL — THIS DEFINES THE STYLE)
Hair must NOT look real.

The hair is sculpted:
• carved locks and grooves
• thick grouped strands
• simplified shapes
• visible chisel cuts
• rigid structure
• no flyaways, no softness, no realistic strands

Think: artisan statue hair, not human hair.

CLOTHING
Clothing becomes carved fabric:
• simplified folds
• hardened drapery
• painted texture
• slightly worn edges

COMPOSITION
• chest-up bust
• mounted on a round pedestal base
• centered framing
• neutral studio background
• soft museum lighting
• photographed like an art catalog

AVOID
real skin texture
photoreal pores
```

SCENE:
A trading settlement built around a large stone bridge crossing a deep river gorge with shops, storage sheds, and stairways leading to dock platforms below. Tiny traders move goods while birds glide along canyon walls.
STYLE:
Create a premium stylized miniature diorama where canyon terrain and river water form a continuous sculpted base integrated with market structures. The entire diorama floats in mid-air inside a blank single-color background environment that contrasts with the rocky terrain. Use stylized resin water, compact shops, and rope docks. Include miniature traders, carts, birds, barrels, crates, and rope details to reinforce handcrafted miniature storytelling scale. Lock the render to 4:3.
LIGHTING:
The scene occurs in late evening after sunset with very low natural light. Ambient lighting remains dim while lanterns, shop lights, and small lamps illuminate the bridge and market stalls. These lights create warm glowing pockets of illumination across the trading post while surrounding canyon surfaces remain darker, producing strong contrast and dramatic miniature depth.
CAMERA:
Use an isometric camera capturing the entire floating diorama clearly from top to bottom and side to side.

### 88. 樱花停车场肖像提示

**Author**: [Danna R.](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-03-05  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的超写实肖像提示，用于生成一张主体坐在停车场石墙上，周围有樱花的图像，强调基于自拍的身份锁定和特定的技术相机设置（iPhone 17 Pro 模拟，35mm，f/8）。

```
(9:16) Photorealistic medium-wide environmental portrait, iPhone 17 Pro sim, 35mm, f/8, everything sharp, authentic digital grain.

Subject seated on stone wall (~50% frame), camera ~3m. Upper frame: overcast sky + cherry blossom canopy (~40%). Lower frame: concrete parking lot (~20%).

IDENTITY LOCK — inherit ALL permanent facial features from selfie (face shape, bone structure, eyes, nose, lips, chin, skin tone, hair color/texture, freckles/moles/distinct marks). Natural skin detail: micro-pores, vellus hair, soft luminosity, even tone, subtle jaw shadow, nasal highlight, zygomatic light, defined lashes/brows, bright teeth, groomed hair strands.

Expression: pensive, serene; head turned left, gaze upper-left (~45° off-camera); relaxed closed lips.

Hair: inherit selfie color/texture; long voluminous wavy blowout, center part, hair flowing back from face.

Outfit: pale {argument name="dress color" default="mint-blue"} rib-knit sleeveless maxi dress, scoop neckline, ribbed texture, defined S-curve silhouette (+20% waist-hip emphasis).

Pose: sitting on weathered stone retaining wall, torso angled left; right hand holding white smartphone outward; left hand on thigh. White quilted shoulder bag beside subject.

### 92. 瑞典肉丸美食立体书透视模型

**Author**: [AidarosGo](https://x.com/aidarosgo3)  **Date**: 2026-03-05  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化、代码般的提示，用于 Gemini Nano Banana 3 生成一个微型立体模型（1:87 比例），展示传统瑞典肉丸（Köttbullar）以烹饪立体书的形式呈现。该提示通过三个部分详细描述了场景：起源（森林/自然）、转化（烹饪炉灶）和最终的盛宴（摆盘），强调移轴摄影和舒适的斯堪的纳维亚美学。

![瑞典肉丸美食立体书透视模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716090_aukdch_HCqrAeYasAAbU9j.jpg)
![瑞典肉丸美食立体书透视模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716147_fn45l6_HCqq6BNWkAEscMd.jpg)

```
class Culinary_PopUp_Book:
    def __init__(self, dish="Köttbullar (Traditional Swedish Meatballs)"):
        self.base = "Ancient leather-bound cookbook, open on a rustic wooden table"
        self.scale = "1:87 (HO Scale) Miniature Diorama"
        
    def generate_spread(self):
        # 1. Left Page: The Origin (Nature)
        origin_biome = "Dense Swedish pine forest with wild lingonberry bushes and misty green pastures for cattle"
        harvesters = "Miniature foragers picking bright red lingonberries in the woods and traditional farmers tending to dairy cows"
        
        # 2. Center Gutter: The Transformation (Cooking)
        machinery = "Classic Swedish wood stove (vedspis) with a massive, sizzling cast-iron skillet"
        physics = "Rich buttery steam and savory smoke rising from the glowing embers in the gutter"
        
        # 3. Right Page: The Result (Feast)
        plating = f"A massive, delicious pile of finished {dish} swimming in rich brown cream sauce (gräddsås), alongside buttery mashed potatoes"
        garnish = "Miniature chefs carefully placing sprigs of fresh dill and dolloping bright lingonberry jam"
        
        return [origin_biome, machinery, plating, harvesters, garnish]

# EXECUTE RENDER: 8k resolution, tilt-shift photography, warm rustic lighting, cozy Scandinavian aesthetic (Hygge).
```

[[Culinary Diorama]]

### 97. 国家公园步道地图微缩生态系统立体模型

**Author**: [Alexandra Aisling](https://x.com/AllaAisling)  **Date**: 2026-03-05  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Firefly 中的 Nano Banana 2 设计的详细模板提示，旨在生成一张国家公园步道地图在野餐桌上展开的图像，并逐渐演变成一个可探索的微型生态系统立体模型。该提示使用占位符（如 {TRAILHEAD}、{WILDLIFE_1}）进行自定义，并指定了海拔变化、天气和光照（黄金时段的偏远地区光线）等元素。

![国家公园步道地图微缩生态系统立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716690_e5o1re_HCqabmGW4AAVCJ4.jpg)
![国家公园步道地图微缩生态系统立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716517_6ljg89_HCqaomWXcAA7_p0.jpg)
![国家公园步道地图微缩生态系统立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716591_rwkcwo_HCqaLJFaUAIOf_m.jpg)
![国家公园步道地图微缩生态系统立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778717673_ywc88n_HCqa3tfW8AELheo.jpg)

```

### 108. 高速摄像机急速运动提示

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2026-03-05  **Language**: en

> 一段用于视频生成（Kling 3.0）的详细运动提示词，描述了一个单一的连续镜头：镜头从高处开始，向下俯冲，以快速移动和运动模糊穿过一个环境，然后急剧减速，最终聚焦在一个主体上。该提示词详细说明了摄像机运动、动作和风格，旨在营造一种惊险刺激的效果。

```
Motion Prompt: CAMERA:
Single continuous shot. The camera moves at high speed through the environment in a straight-line rush. Starts high above, then immediately dives down into the scene. The camera weaves between obstacles with tight margins — quick banking turns, rapid dodges, surroundings rushing past in peripheral blur. Light flickers rapidly through beams and shadows. Final approach decelerates sharply as the subject comes into view, the speed resolving into a calm, steady hover. Camera settles into a low-angle medium shot with subtle drift.
ACTION:
Opens from above, then plunges into the environment. Surroundings become a blur of color and light streaks. Obstacles whoosh past on both sides, particles streak through the frame. Volumetric light rays flash by. As the subject appears ahead, speed suddenly drops, chaos calms, and the camera floats the final distance. The final frame holds steady on the subject, glowing and still. Nothing is visible in the frame except the environment and the subject.
STYLE:
Thrilling high-speed camera rush. Urgent and exhilarating. Rapid light–shadow transitions with motion blur emphasizing speed. The contrast between the frenetic journey and the calm arrival creates a satisfying effect. CAMERA:
Single continuous shot. The camera moves at high speed through the environment in a straight-line rush. Starts high above, then immediately dives down into the scene. The camera weaves between obstacles with tight margins — quick banking turns, rapid dodges, surroundings rushing past in peripheral blur. Light flickers rapidly through beams and shadows. Final approach decelerates sharply as the subject comes into view, the speed resolving into a calm, steady hover. Camera settles into a low-angle medium shot with subtle drift.
ACTION:
Opens from above, then plunges into the environment. Surroundings become a blur of color and light streaks. Obstacles whoosh past on both sides, particles streak through the frame. Volumetric light rays flash by. As the subject appears ahead, speed suddenly drops, chaos calms, and the camera floats the final distance. The final frame holds steady on the subject, glowing and still. Nothing is visible in the frame except the environment and the subject.
STYLE:

- The Negative Space: Dust motes caught in light rays, following the mathematical curve downward.

```
Create a branded technical infographic of a {argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT NAME"}, fully matching the visual density, structure, and engineering-style presentation of the technical food schematics of {argument name="product name 2" default="PRODUCT NAME"} with all text written in English
CRITICAL LANGUAGE RULE: Every visible word on the image must be in English.
Visual Concept
A realistic photograph or photorealistic render of the snack combined with dense technical annotation overlays, exactly like an engineering or food-packaging blueprint. Pure white studio background.
Required Technical Elements (ALL LABELED IN English)
• Labels for key product components • Internal cross-section showing structure, layers, or filling • Measurements: height, width, volume, weight (metric system) • Packaging and product material callouts with composition and quantities • Arrows indicating function, pressure, sealing, and structural integrity • Simple schematic or sectional diagram of mechanics / form / packaging • Sustainability and environmental callouts (recycling, materials, waste reduction)
Title Placement
Product name in English, bold font, inside a hand-drawn technical annotation frame (as in engineering blueprints), positioned in the upper corner.
Style & Layout
• Very high information density • Annotations feel like an engineering / architectural sketch • Black lines — 70–80% of all graphics • Accent {argument name="brand color" default="BRAND COLOR"} — 20–30% (arrows, key zones, headings) • The realistic product remains fully readable • Educational, food-engineering, industrial-premium aesthetic • Small brand logo in the corner (in English)
Visual Style
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic: black linework over realistic imagery, precise, highly detailed, slightly hand-drawn, like professional technical manuals.
Color Palette
White background Black text and linework {argument name="brand color 2" default="BRAND COLOR"} used only for accents
Output
9:16 Vertical portrait, 8K, highly detailed,  Ultra-crisp image Social-feed optimized No watermark
```

```
Create a branded technical infographic of a [{argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT NAME"}], fully matching the visual density, structure, and engineering-style presentation of the technical food schematics of [PRODUCT NAME]with all text written in English
CRITICAL LANGUAGE RULE: Every visible word on the image must be in English.
Visual Concept
A realistic photograph or photorealistic render of the snack combined with dense technical annotation overlays, exactly like an engineering or food-packaging blueprint. Pure white studio background.
Required Technical Elements (ALL LABELED IN English)
• Labels for key product components • Internal cross-section showing structure, layers, or filling • Measurements: height, width, volume, weight (metric system) • Packaging and product material callouts with composition and quantities • Arrows indicating function, pressure, sealing, and structural integrity • Simple schematic or sectional diagram of mechanics / form / packaging • Sustainability and environmental callouts (recycling, materials, waste reduction)
Title Placement
Product name in English, bold font, inside a hand-drawn technical annotation frame (as in engineering blueprints), positioned in the upper corner.
Style & Layout
• Very high information density • Annotations feel like an engineering / architectural sketch • Black lines — 70–80% of all graphics • Accent [{argument name="brand color" default="BRAND COLOR"}] — 20–30% (arrows, key zones, headings) • The realistic product remains fully readable • Educational, food-engineering, industrial-premium aesthetic • Small brand logo in the corner (in English)
Visual Style
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic: black linework over realistic imagery, precise, highly detailed, slightly hand-drawn, like professional technical manuals.
Color Palette
White background Black text and linework [BRAND COLOR] used only for accents
Output
9:16 Vertical portrait, 8K, highly detailed,  Ultra-crisp image Social-feed optimized No watermark

### 171. 电影感时尚肖像，带动态模糊鬼影效果

          "prismatic light refraction",
          "soft caustic highlights"
        ]

    },

        "anodized brushed aluminum with micro-circular grain",

      ],

    },

        "no platforms",
        "no props",

        "no background gradients"
      ],

### 183. Nano Banana Pro 健身社论网格提示（黄色运动服，身份锁定）

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: en

> 这是一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 模型的高度具体的 JSON 提示，旨在生成一个 2x2 的编辑健身拼贴画，其中所有四个画面都展现同一位女性运动员。它指定了四种不同的姿势、浅柔和的黄色运动服主题，并对解剖结构和手部有严格的质量控制，使用图像到图像模式来保持身份一致性。

![Nano Banana Pro 健身社论网格提示（黄色运动服，身份锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692215482_s86ypg_HClZ55iWcAARfh5.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "fitness_editorial_2x2_pose_grid_identity_locked",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v2.0_YELLOW_FITNESS_EDITORIAL_GRID"
    },

    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "maximum",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "notes": "Create a 2x2 editorial fitness collage using the four reference poses: (1) floor bicycle crunch pose, (2) deep forward fold stretch, (3) kneeling back stretch pose, (4) standing dumbbell pose. Same woman identity in all frames."
    },

    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "outer_border": "none"
      },
      "sharpness": "editorial_crisp",
      "grain": "subtle_film",
      "render_style": "premium_fitness_editorial"
    },

    "styling": {
      "outfit": {
        "top": "light pastel yellow athletic sports bra",
        "bottom": "light pastel yellow seamless leggings",
        "fabric": "matte performance fabric"
      },
      "shoes": "light pastel yellow running sneakers matching the outfit",
      "socks": "white athletic crew socks",
      "headphones": "light pastel yellow over-ear fitness headphones",
      "dumbbells": "light pastel yellow coated dumbbells",
      "color_palette": [
        "soft pastel yellow",
        "warm neutral skin tones",
        "clean studio white background"
      ]
    },

    "scene": {
      "environment": "minimal clean studio background, soft white / light beige tone",
      "lighting": "soft high-end fitness studio lighting, even highlights, clean shadows",
      "camera": {
        "lens": "50mm",
        "focus": "sharp on subject with subtle depth",
        "composition": "editorial sports campaign style"
      }
    },

      "hands_priority": "high",
      "finger_count": 5,
      "correct_thumb_orientation": true,
      "natural_muscle_definition": true,
      "no_extra_limbs": true,
      "no_distortion": true
    },

    "quality_control": {
      "avoid": [
        "logos",
        "text",
        "brand names",
        "watermark",
        "extra fingers",
        "missing fingers",
        "distorted anatomy",
        "plastic skin",
        "blurry face"
      ]

      "text",

### 185. 电影级 360 度环绕跟踪镜头视频提示

**Author**: [MotionViz](https://x.com/Motion_Viz)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，用于使用 Nano Banana Pro 和 Kling 3.0 生成一个 10 秒的电影视频，其中包含一个围绕中心人物以力量姿势进行的 360 度旋转轨道跟踪镜头，强调运动一致性和空间锚定的技术细节。

```
Cinematic 360-degree rotating orbital tracking shot. The camera maintains an low-angle "worm's-eye view" while rotating in a full circle around the central character. The character remains in a powerful, wide-stanced power pose, holding the massive rusted chain-wrapped spear vertically. As the camera orbits, the futuristic white circular laboratory environment rotates seamlessly in the background. High-fidelity textures on the black leather tactical boots, the puffy grey jacket, and the weathered metal of the spear. Photorealistic lighting with subtle lens flares from the overhead circular lights. Consistent character features, maintaining the beanie and silver necklaces throughout the rotation. Smooth, stabilized 10-second motion path. 8k resolution, highly detailed, IMAX aesthetic.

Logic and Composition Breakdown
Spatial Anchoring
For a 360 spin to work on a website hero section, the axis of rotation must be the spear and the character’s midline. By specifying "orbital tracking shot," you instruct the AI to move the camera on a circular track rather than just spinning the image, which prevents "melting" or warping of the character's limbs.

Consistency Mapping
Primary Anchor: The rusted, chain-wrapped spear. Its central position in the frame acts as the pivot point.

Secondary Anchor: The oversized tactical boots. Their placement at the bottom corners of the frame must remain grounded on the white grid floor to prevent "floating" during the spin.

Environment: The circular ceiling lights provide a natural geometric guide for the AI to calculate the rotation vector.

Technical Parameters for Kling 3.0 Pro
Motion Sensitivity: Set to 5 or 6. High enough to complete the rotation, but low enough to avoid limb deformation.

Prompt Weighting: Focus on "Rotation" and "Orbital" to ensure the camera completes a full circle within the 10-second duration.

Negative Prompt
Distorted facial features, morphing limbs, spear changing shape, boots losing detail, background flickering, jerky camera movement, zoom-in, zoom-out, character walking, changing clothes, blurry textures, low resolution, 2D anime style, cartoonish, floating objects, extra fingers, messy hair.
```

[[Video Generation Workflow]]

### 199. Vlog 风格视频生成提示，适用于 Nano Banana Pro 和 Google Veo 3.1（重复）

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个逼真、高质量、Vlog 风格的视频，内容是一位女性讨论时尚。该提示详细说明了摄像机角度、灯光、构图、情绪、对话和背景音乐，以实现一种亲密、未经剪辑的观感。（这是推文 2029059260647391712 的副本）。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Video Generation Workflow]]

### 200. Vlog 风格视频生成提示语，适用于 Nano Banana Pro 和 Google Veo 3.1

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-03-04  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个逼真、高质量、Vlog 风格的视频，内容是一位女性讨论时尚。该提示详细说明了摄像机角度、灯光、构图、情绪、对话和背景音乐，以实现一种亲密、未经剪辑的观感。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```
